LLM提示注入风险: 代码将用户控制的response和task_context直接嵌入到LLM提示 (RAG-7eb192c6)

high

位置: C:\1AAA_PROJECT\HOS\HOS-LS\real-project\nanobot-0.1.4.post6\bridge\tsconfig.json:1

SSRF防护绕过风险 (NETWORK-001)

medium

位置: C:\1AAA_PROJECT\HOS\HOS-LS\real-project\nanobot-0.1.4.post6\nanobot\security\network.py:38

描述: validate_url_target函数存在SSRF防护绕过风险，攻击者可能通过DNS重绑定、IPv6地址、特殊域名解析等方式绕过内部地址检测

置信度: 0.75

def validate_url_target(url: str) -> tuple[bool, str]: """Validate a URL is safe to fetch: scheme, hostname, and resolved IPs. Returns (ok, error_message). When ok is True, error_message is empty. """ try: p = urlparse(url) except Exception as e: return False, str(e) if p.scheme not in ("http", "https"): return False, f"Only http/https allowed, got '{p.scheme or 'none'}'" if not p.netloc: return False, "Missing domain" hostname = p.hostname if not hostname: return False, "Missing hostname" try: infos = socket.getaddrinfo(hostname, None, socket.AF_UNSPEC, socket.SOCK_STREAM) except socket.gaierror: return False, f"Cannot resolve hostname: {hostname}" for info in infos: try: addr = ipaddress.ip_address(info[4][0]) except ValueError: continue if _is_private(addr): return False, f"Blocked: {hostname} resolves to private/internal address {addr}" return True, ""

修复建议: 1. 添加DNS解析超时限制，防止DNS重绑定攻击 2. 考虑使用白名单机制替代黑名单 3. 添加对IPv6压缩格式和特殊地址的检测 4. 实现DNS解析缓存，防止同一域名多次解析返回不同结果 5. 添加对URL编码、特殊字符的规范化处理

ws.once('message', (data) => { clearTimeout(timeout); try { const msg = JSON.parse(data.toString()); if (msg.type === 'auth' && msg.token === this.token) { console.log('🔗 Python client authenticated'); this.setupClient(ws); } else { ws.close(4003, 'Invalid token'); } } catch { ws.close(4003, 'Invalid auth message'); } });

路径遍历漏洞 (FS-001)

medium

位置: C:\1AAA_PROJECT\HOS\HOS-LS\real-project\nanobot-0.1.4.post6\nanobot\agent\tools\filesystem.py:13

描述: _resolve_path函数中的路径解析逻辑可能被绕过，导致访问受限目录之外的文件

置信度: 0.7

def _resolve_path( path: str, workspace: Path | None = None, allowed_dir: Path | None = None, extra_allowed_dirs: list[Path] | None = None, ) -> Path: """Resolve path against workspace (if relative) and enforce directory restriction.""" p = Path(path).expanduser() if not p.is_absolute() and workspace: p = workspace / p resolved = p.resolve() if allowed_dir: all_dirs = [allowed_dir] + (extra_allowed_dirs or []) if not any(_is_under(resolved, d) for d in all_dirs): raise PermissionError(f"Path {path} is outside allowed directory {allowed_dir}") return resolved

修复建议: 1. 在路径解析前进行规范化处理，移除路径中的'..'和符号链接 2. 使用pathlib的resolve(strict=True)确保解析后的路径是规范化的 3. 添加额外的路径验证，如检查路径是否包含'..'或绝对路径绕过 4. 考虑使用os.path.normpath进行路径规范化
